  <h4 class="h5-mktg color-fg-default mb-2 col-11">Code owners</h4>
  <p class="color-fg-muted f4 col-9 mb-1">
    Automatically request reviews–or require approval—by selected contributors when changes are made to sections of code that they own.
  </p>
    <a class="link-mktg text-semibold color-fg-default py-1 color-fg-accent f4-mktg" href="https://docs.github.com/en/github/creating-cloning-and-archiving-repositories/about-code-owners" data-analytics-event="{&quot;category&quot;:&quot;Features&quot;,&quot;action&quot;:&quot;click to learn more about Code owners&quot;,&quot;label&quot;:&quot;ref_page:/features;ref_cta:Learn more;ref_loc:collaborative coding category&quot;}">

  <p class="color-fg-muted f4 col-9 mb-1">

<div class="js-unveil-item features-category-item col-12 col-md-6 col-lg-4 mb-6 mb-md-8">
  <h4 class="h5-mktg color-fg-default mb-2 col-11">Secret scanning</h4>
  <p class="color-fg-muted f4 col-9 mb-1">
    Find secrets hard-coded in your public and private repositories. Revoke them to keep access to the services you use secure.
  </p>

  <h4 class="h5-mktg color-fg-default mb-2 col-11">IP allow list</h4>
  <p class="color-fg-muted f4 col-9 mb-1">
    Limit access to enterprise assets to an allowed set of source IPs. The allow list will block access for any IP addresses not included via the web, API, and Git.

      <h2 class="h2-mktg features-category--title">Community</h2>

      <div class="d-flex col-md-4 pb-5 pb-md-0 mb-5 flex-justify-between">
  <a class="d-flex flex-column flex-justify-between no-underline box-shadow-card-border-mktg rounded-2 width-full resource-card arrow-target-mktg color-bg-subtle p-4" href="/marketplace">
    
    <img class="mb-3 box-shadow-card-mktg circle" width="64" height="64" loading="lazy" decoding="async" alt="" src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/modules/site/features/launchpad/icons/icon-github-marketplace.svg" />
